    $(function () {
        var
                ui5ico = '.ui5ico',
                $ui5ico = $(ui5ico),
                ui5icoStyle = [];

        $ui5ico.each(function () {
            var
                    ui5icoDataName = 'data-ui5ico',
                    ui5icoContent = $(this).attr(ui5icoDataName).toLowerCase().trim(),
                    ui5icoDataSelector = ui5ico + '[' + ui5icoDataName + '=' + ui5icoContent + ']';

            if (ui5icoContent.startsWith('x')) {
                var ui5icoContent = ui5icoContent.replace('x', '');
            }

            var
                    ui5icoContent = '"\\' + ui5icoContent + '"',
                    ui5icoCSSRule = ui5icoDataSelector + ':before{content:' + ui5icoContent + '!important;}';

            if (ui5icoStyle.includes(ui5icoCSSRule) == false) {
                ui5icoStyle.push(ui5icoCSSRule);
            }
        });

        var
                ui5icoStyle = ui5icoStyle.join(''),
                ui5icoStyle = '<style type="text/css">' + ui5icoStyle + '</style>';

        $('head').append(ui5icoStyle);
    });
</script>

<script type='text/javascript'>
    function myFunction() {
        var topbar = document.getElementsByClassName("nav-pills");
        var langLink = document.getElementsByClassName("languageselector");
        var langList = document.getElementsByClassName("headerdropdown");
        var profile = document.getElementsByClassName("profileWidget").children;
        var list1 = document.createElement("li");
        var list2 = document.createElement("li");

        list1.classList.add("custom-menu-item1");
        list2.classList.add("custom-menu-item2");
        list1.appendChild(langLink);
        list1.appendChild(langList);
        list2.appendChild(profile);

        topbar.appendChild(list1);
        topbar.appendChild(list2);
    }
    //window.onload = myFunction;

			<script type="text/javascript">
                //<![CDATA[
                    var addthis_config = {
                        username:'addthisj2w'
                        ,ui_open_windows: true
                        ,ui_click: true
                        ,ui_508_compliant: true
                        ,data_track_clickback: false
                        ,ui_language: "en"
                        ,data_ga_property: ""
                        ,data_ga_social: true
                    };

                    var calledsfshorturl = false;

                    $(function () {
                        var $toolbox = $('.addthis_toolbox');

                        $toolbox.mouseover(function (e) {
                            if (!calledsfshorturl) {
                                calledsfshorturl = true;
                                $(this).sfshorturl({
                                    callback:addthisCallback
                                    ,event:e
                                });
                            }
                        });

                        $toolbox.find('a.addthis_button_pinterest_share').on('click keypress', function (e) {
                            if (e.which === 13 && e.type !== 'click') {
                                $(this).click();
                                e.preventDefault();
                            }

                            if (e.type === 'click') {
                                e.preventDefault();
                            }
                        });

                        function addthisCallback(data) {
                            $(data.event.target).attr('addthis:url',data.shorturl);
                            addthis.update('share', 'url', data.shorturl);
                        }
                    });
                //]]>

    <span xml:lang="en-US" lang="en-US" itemprop="description" data-careersite-propertyid="description">
                <span class="jobdescription"><p><span style="font-size:14.0px"><span style="font-family:Arial, Helvetica, sans-serif"><b>What we offer</b></span></span></p>

<p><span style="font-size:14.0px"><span style="font-family:Arial, Helvetica, sans-serif">Our company culture is focused on helping our employees enable innovation by building breakthroughs together. How? We focus every day on building the foundation for tomorrow and creating a workplace that embraces differences, values flexibility, and is aligned to our purpose-driven and future-focused work. We offer a highly collaborative, caring team environment with a strong focus on learning and development, recognition for your individual contributions, and a variety of benefit options for you to choose from. Apply now!</span></span></p>

<p> </p>

<p> </p>
<p> </p>

<p><b>ROLE DESCRIPTION</b></p>

<p> </p>

<p><span style="font-size:12.0pt"><span style="font-family:Calibri, sans-serif"><span style="font-size:11.5pt"><span style="color:#404040">Do you want to develop products and services that impact thousands of clients and millions of users around the globe? Are you ready to play a key role in defining and implementing services and solutions that have impact across our entire company? Do you dream of delivering excellence and driving innovation? If the answer is yes, then the Cloud Services team at SAP Concur is the place for you.</span></span></span></span></p>

<p><br>
<b><span style="font-size:12.0pt"><span style="font-family:Calibri, sans-serif"><span style="border:none windowtext 1.0pt;font-size:11.5pt;padding:0.0in"><span style="color:#404040">As a Software Developer on our team you will:</span></span></span></span></b></p>

<p> </p>

<ul>
	<li><span style="font-size:12.0pt"><span><span style="vertical-align:baseline"><span style="font-family:Calibri, sans-serif"><span style="font-size:11.5pt"><span style="color:#404040">Solve complex problems and design systems that enable best-in-class operation of SAP Concur’s cloud services and communications with our customers.</span></span></span></span></span></span></li>
	<li><span style="font-size:12.0pt"><span><span style="vertical-align:baseline"><span style="font-family:Calibri, sans-serif"><span style="font-size:11.5pt"><span style="color:#404040">Develop across the full-stack on a variety of technologies including Python/Flask, Node.js/Express, ReactJS, Redux, Docker containers and Kubernetes.</span></span></span></span></span></span></li>
	<li><span style="font-size:12.0pt"><span><span style="vertical-align:baseline"><span style="font-family:Calibri, sans-serif"><span style="font-size:11.5pt"><span style="color:#404040">Leverage the latest and greatest AWS Cloud technologies as you build and innovate.</span></span></span></span></span></span></li>
	<li><span style="font-size:12.0pt"><span><span style="vertical-align:baseline"><span style="font-family:Calibri, sans-serif"><span style="font-size:11.5pt"><span style="color:#404040">Embrace end-to-end ownership and DevOps practices: architect, design, code, test, deploy and monitor your software in providing direct value to our customers.</span></span></span></span></span></span></li>
	<li><span style="font-size:12.0pt"><span><span style="vertical-align:baseline"><span style="font-family:Calibri, sans-serif"><span style="font-size:11.5pt"><span style="color:#404040">Cooperate with other engineers and product owners in an ever-evolving, Agile environment.</span></span></span></span></span></span></li>
	<li><span style="font-size:12.0pt"><span><span style="vertical-align:baseline"><span style="font-family:Calibri, sans-serif"><span style="font-size:11.5pt"><span style="color:#404040">Learn, as we move fast and are unafraid to venture into the unknown.</span></span></span></span></span></span></li>
	<li><span style="font-size:12.0pt"><span><span style="vertical-align:baseline"><span style="font-family:Calibri, sans-serif"><span style="font-size:11.5pt"><span style="color:#404040">Be part of a team that owns products, tools and services that help other teams deliver better software and improve our relationship with customers.</span></span></span></span></span></span></li>
</ul>

<p> </p>

<p><b><span style="font-size:12.0pt"><span><span style="vertical-align:baseline"><span style="font-family:Calibri, sans-serif"><span style="border:none windowtext 1.0pt;font-size:11.5pt;padding:0.0in"><span style="color:#404040">In order to accomplish this you will need:</span></span></span></span></span></span></b></p>

<p> </p>

<ul>
	<li><span style="font-size:12.0pt"><span><span style="vertical-align:baseline"><span style="font-family:Calibri, sans-serif"><span style="font-size:11.5pt"><span style="color:#404040">A solid understanding and experience with software development principles and practices.</span></span></span></span></span></span></li>
	<li><span style="font-size:12.0pt"><span><span style="vertical-align:baseline"><span style="font-family:Calibri, sans-serif"><span style="font-size:11.5pt"><span style="color:#404040">A passion for maintaining high quality, robust and scalable services.</span></span></span></span></span></span></li>
	<li><span style="font-size:12.0pt"><span><span style="vertical-align:baseline"><span style="font-family:Calibri, sans-serif"><span style="font-size:11.5pt"><span style="color:#404040">Attention to details and strive for excellence in the quality of code you produce.</span></span></span></span></span></span></li>
	<li><span style="font-size:12.0pt"><span><span style="vertical-align:baseline"><span style="font-family:Calibri, sans-serif"><span style="font-size:11.5pt"><span style="color:#404040">A high degree of intellectual curiosity and a lack of fear for learning something new. You should be open to learning from others and also willing to share your knowledge with the team.</span></span></span></span></span></span></li>
</ul>

<p> </p>

<p><b><span style="font-size:12.0pt"><span><span style="vertical-align:baseline"><span style="font-family:Calibri, sans-serif"><span style="font-size:11.5pt"><span style="color:#404040">Position Requirements</span></span></span></span></span></span></b></p>

<p> </p>

<ul>
	<li><span style="font-size:12.0pt"><span><span><span style="vertical-align:baseline"><span style="font-family:Calibri, sans-serif"><span style="font-size:11.5pt"><span style="color:#404040">BS  in Computer Science, Computer Engineering or related field</span></span></span></span></span></span></span></li>
	<li><span style="font-size:12.0pt"><span><span><span style="vertical-align:baseline"><span style="font-family:Calibri, sans-serif"><span style="font-size:11.5pt"><span style="color:#404040">2+ years of software development experience with a solid understanding of the full software stack</span></span></span></span></span></span></span></li>
	<li><span style="font-size:12.0pt"><span><span><span style="vertical-align:baseline"><span style="font-family:Calibri, sans-serif"><span style="font-size:11.5pt"><span style="color:#404040">Proven experience coding object-oriented and modularized software</span></span></span></span></span></span></span></li>
	<li><span style="font-size:12.0pt"><span><span><span style="vertical-align:baseline"><span style="font-family:Calibri, sans-serif"><span style="font-size:11.5pt"><span style="color:#404040">Experience building scalable, reliable and high-performing software systems</span></span></span></span></span></span></span></li>
	<li><span style="font-size:12.0pt"><span><span><span style="vertical-align:baseline"><span style="font-family:Calibri, sans-serif"><span style="font-size:11.5pt"><span style="color:#404040">Solid Linux and/or Unix skills</span></span></span></span></span></span></span></li>
	<li><span style="font-size:12.0pt"><span><span><span style="vertical-align:baseline"><span style="font-family:Calibri, sans-serif"><span style="font-size:11.5pt"><span style="color:#404040">Experience with RESTful API design and service operation</span></span></span></span></span></span></span></li>
	<li><span style="font-size:12.0pt"><span><span><span style="vertical-align:baseline"><span style="font-family:Calibri, sans-serif"><span style="font-size:11.5pt"><span style="color:#404040">Working knowledge of databases (SQL, NoSQL, Document)</span></span></span></span></span></span></span></li>
	<li><span style="font-size:12.0pt"><span><span><span style="vertical-align:baseline"><span style="font-family:Calibri, sans-serif"><span style="font-size:11.5pt"><span style="color:#404040">Experience with AWS as well as container technologies/Kubernetes</span></span></span></span></span></span></span></li>
	<li><span style="font-size:12.0pt"><span><span><span style="vertical-align:baseline"><span style="font-family:Calibri, sans-serif"><span style="font-size:11.5pt"><span style="color:#404040">Must have excellent verbal and communication skills</span></span></span></span></span></span></span></li>
</ul>

<p><br>
<b><span style="font-size:12.0pt"><span><span style="vertical-align:baseline"><span style="font-family:Calibri, sans-serif"><span style="font-size:11.5pt"><span style="color:#404040"><span style="border:none windowtext 1.0pt;padding:0.0in">So who are we?<u> </u></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></b></p>

<p><br>
<span style="font-size:12.0pt"><span><span style="vertical-align:baseline"><span style="font-family:Calibri, sans-serif"><span style="font-size:11.5pt"><span style="color:#404040">SAP Concur imagines the way the world should work, offering cloud-based services that make it simple to manage travel and expenses. Founded in 1993, SAP Concur services are used by 30,000 clients representing 27 million users in more than 150 countries.</span></span></span></span></span></span><br>
 </p>

<p> </p>
<p> </p>

<p> </p>

<p><span style="font-size:14.0px"><span style="font-family:Arial, Helvetica, sans-serif"><b>We are SAP</b></span></span></p>

<p><span style="font-size:14.0px"><span style="font-family:Arial, Helvetica, sans-serif">SAP innovations help more than 400,000 customers worldwide work together more efficiently and use business insight more effectively. Originally known for leadership in enterprise resource planning (ERP) software, SAP has evolved to become a market leader in end-to-end business application software and related services for database, analytics, intelligent technologies, and experience management. As a cloud company with 200 million users and more than 100,000 employees worldwide, we are purpose-driven and future-focused, with a highly collaborative team ethic and commitment to personal development. Whether connecting global industries, people, or platforms, we help ensure every challenge gets the solution it deserves. At SAP, we build breakthroughs, together.</span></span></p>

<p> </p>

<p><span style="font-size:14.0px"><span style="font-family:Arial, Helvetica, sans-serif"><b>Our inclusion promise </b></span></span></p>

At SAP, we believe we are made stronger by the unique capabilities and qualities that each person brings to our company, and we invest in our employees to inspire confidence and help everyone realize their full potential. We ultimately believe in unleashing all talent and creating a better and more equitable world.</span></span></p>

<script type="text/javascript">
        $(function(){
            $(".job-location").detach().appendTo(".jobdescription");
        });
    function equalHeight() {
        var
                $e = $('#carousel .item'),
                _a = [];

        $e.each(function () {
            $(this).addClass('active').css('min-height', 0);
            var h = $(this).outerHeight(true);
            _a.push(h);
        });

        var x = Math.max.apply(Math, _a);

        $e.each(function (i) {
            if (i !== 0) {
                $(this).removeClass('active');
            }
            $(this).css('min-height', x);
        });
    }

    $(window).on({
        'load': function () {
            equalHeight();
        },
        'resize': function () {
            equalHeight();
        }
    });
</script>

			<script type="text/javascript">
                //<![CDATA[
                    var addthis_config = {
                        username:'addthisj2w'
                        ,ui_open_windows: true
                        ,ui_click: true
                        ,ui_508_compliant: true
                        ,data_track_clickback: false
                        ,ui_language: "en"

                    var calledsfshorturl = false;

                    $(function () {
                        var $toolbox = $('.addthis_toolbox');

                        $toolbox.mouseover(function (e) {
                            if (!calledsfshorturl) {
                                calledsfshorturl = true;
                                $(this).sfshorturl({
                                    callback:addthisCallback
                                    ,event:e
                                });
                            }
                        });

                        $toolbox.find('a.addthis_button_pinterest_share').on('click keypress', function (e) {
                            if (e.which === 13 && e.type !== 'click') {
                                $(this).click();
                                e.preventDefault();
                            }

                            if (e.type === 'click') {
                                e.preventDefault();
                            }
                        });

                        function addthisCallback(data) {
                            $(data.event.target).attr('addthis:url',data.shorturl);
                            addthis.update('share', 'url', data.shorturl);
                        }
                    });
                //]]>

    $(function(){
        function stickyFontChange(){
            var width = $(window).width(); 
            var height = $(window).height(); 
            if (width >= 1024) {
                jQuery(".jobColumnTwo").children().css("padding", "14px 24px" );
                jQuery("#similar-jobs").children().css("font-size", "16px" );
                jQuery(".subscribe-frequency-label").children().css("font-size", "16px" );
            } else{
                jQuery(".jobColumnTwo").children().css("padding", "8px 24px" );
                jQuery("#similar-jobs").children().css("font-size", "16px" );
                jQuery(".subscribe-frequency-label").children().css("font-size", "16px" );
            }
            if (height >= 870) {
                jQuery(".jobColumnTwo").children().css("padding", "14px 24px" );
            } else if (height>= 760) {
                jQuery(".jobColumnTwo").children().css("padding", "8px 24px" );
            } else if (height>= 722) {
                jQuery(".jobColumnTwo").children().css("padding", "4px 24px" );
            } else {
                jQuery(".jobColumnTwo").children().css("padding", "2px 24px" );
            }
            if (width <= 1024 && height >= 945) {
                jQuery(".jobColumnTwo").children().css("padding", "14px 24px" );
            } else if (width <= 1024 && height >= 855) {
                jQuery(".jobColumnTwo").children().css("padding", "8px 24px" );
            } else if (width <= 1024 && height >= 794) {
                jQuery(".jobColumnTwo").children().css("padding", "4px 24px" );
            }
            if (width <= 800 && height >= 1040) {
                jQuery(".jobColumnTwo").children().css("padding", "14px 24px" );
            } else if (width <= 800  && height >= 935) {
                jQuery(".jobColumnTwo").children().css("padding", "8px 24px" );
            } else if (width <= 800  && height >= 874) {
                jQuery(".jobColumnTwo").children().css("padding", "4px 24px" );
            }
        }
        stickyFontChange();
        $(window).resize(function(){
            stickyFontChange();
        });
        $(window).scroll(function(){
            stickyFontChange();
        });
    });
</script>

    $(function () {
        function sideBar() {
            if (window.location.href.indexOf('/job/') > -1) {
                var width = $(window).width();
                var height = $(window).height();
                var scrollTop = $(window).scrollTop(),

                        responsiveValue = getComputedStyle(document.querySelector('body'), ':before').getPropertyValue('content').replace(/"/g, ''),

                        container = '.jobDisplayShell .jobDisplay .job',
                        element = container + ' ' + '.jobColumnTwo',
                        defaultOffset = 180,

                        containerOffsetTop = $(container).offset().top,
                        containerHeight = $(container).outerHeight(true),

                        elementHeight = $(element).outerHeight(true),
                        elementSpace = defaultOffset + elementHeight,

                        distanceTop = containerOffsetTop - scrollTop,

                        upperBoundary = defaultOffset,
                        lowerBoundary = elementSpace - containerHeight;

                /*
                 console.log('responsiveValue == ' + responsiveValue);
                 console.log('screen.height == ' + screen.height);
                 console.log('$(#header).height() == ' + $('#header').height());
                 console.log('containerHeight == ' + containerHeight);
                 console.log('elementHeight == ' + elementHeight);
                 console.log('$(window).height() == ' + $(window).height());
                 */

                if (responsiveValue == 'mobile') {
                    $(element).removeClass(responsiveValue);
                    return;
                }

                if ((!$(element).hasClass('noScroll')) && (distanceTop <= upperBoundary) && (distanceTop >= lowerBoundary)) {
                    $(element).addClass('noScroll');
                    $(element).removeClass('scrollTop');
                    $(element).removeClass('scrollBottom');
                }
                if ((!$(element).hasClass('scrollTop')) && distanceTop > upperBoundary) {
                    $(element).removeClass('noScroll');
                    $(element).addClass('scrollTop');
                    $(element).removeClass('scrollBottom');
                }
                if ((!$(element).hasClass('scrollBottom')) && distanceTop < lowerBoundary) {
                    $(element).removeClass('noScroll');
                    $(element).removeClass('scrollTop');
                    $(element).addClass('scrollBottom');
                }
            }
        };

        $(window).resize(function () {
            sideBar();
        });

        $(window).scroll(function () {
            sideBar();
        });
    });
    $(function () {
        jQuery(".row.videocomponent.videocomponent1d171fc0d122882d.backgroundcolor4af43e749de8e90f.linkcolor6dbb99856a7f4c83.linkhovercolor6dbb99856a7f4c83.displayDTM ").detach().appendTo('.second-grid-container');
        jQuery(".row.videocomponent.videocomponentf96c787b5d22266e.backgroundcolor1f69358334761fba.linkcolor6dbb99856a7f4c83.linkhovercolor6dbb99856a7f4c83.displayDTM ").detach().appendTo('.second-grid-container');
        jQuery(".row.videocomponent.videocomponent3b7d320da14eb937.backgroundcolorf502b1e6c2567c38.linkcolor6dbb99856a7f4c83.linkhovercolor6dbb99856a7f4c83.displayDTM ").detach().appendTo('.second-grid-container');
        function jobColChange() {
            var width = $(window).width();
            var height = $(window).height();
            if (width >= 768) {
                $(".jobColumnTwo").detach().appendTo('.job');
                $(".second-grid-container").css("width", "");
                $(".second-grid-container").css("padding", "0px");
                $(".second-grid-container").detach().appendTo('.jobColumnOne');
                $(".jobColumnOne").css("border-right", "1px solid rgba(0, 0, 0, 0.0)");
                $(".holdJobColTwo").css("display", "grid");
                $(".jobColumnTwo").css("height", "100vh");
                $(".jobColumnTwo").css("padding-top", "0px");
            } else {
                $(".jobColumnTwo").detach().appendTo('.jobColumnOne');
                $(".second-grid-container").detach().appendTo('.job');
                $(".second-grid-container").css("width", "100%");
                $(".second-grid-container").css("padding", "0px !important");
                $(".jobColumnOne").css("border-right", "none");
                $(".jobColumnTwo").css("-webkit-box-shadow", "none");
                $(".jobColumnTwo").css("-moz-box-shadow", "none");
                $(".jobColumnTwo").css("box-shadow", "none");
                $(".jobColumnTwo").css("height", "");
                $(".jobColumnTwo").detach().appendTo('.job');
                $(".jobColumnTwo").css("padding-top", "15px");
                $(".holdJobColTwo").css("display", "none");
            }
        }

        jobColChange();
        $(window).resize(function () {
            jobColChange();
        });
    });
</script>

    /* A function to adjust the size of the first column depending on the screen size */
    $(function(){
        function jobColumnOneChange(){
            var width = $(window).width(); 
            var height = $(window).height(); 
            if (width >= 768){
                $('.jobColumnOne').css('padding-right', '2%');
            } else if (width >= 480){
                $('.jobColumnOne').css('padding-right', '5%');
            } else{
                $('.jobColumnOne').css('padding-right', '5%');
            }
        }

        /* Call the above function on page load, on page resize, and on page scroll */
        jobColumnOneChange();

        $(window).resize(function(){
            jobColumnOneChange();
        });
        $(window).scroll(function(){
            jobColumnOneChange();
        });
    });
</script>

        <div class="inner"><style>
    .bh-survey {
        top: 180px;
    }
    .bh-survey-sticky-btn {
        position: absolute !important;
        top: 73% !important;
    }
    .bh-survey-sticky-btn-2 {
        position: fixed !important;

    .bh-survey-sticky-btn-3 {

    <script type="text/javascript">
        $.fn.jobColumnOneInViewport = function() {
            var top = $('.jobColumnOne').offset().top;
            return ($(document).scrollTop() + $('#header').outerHeight(true)) >= top-5;
        };
        $.fn.jobColumnTwoInViewport = function() {
            var top = $('.jobColumnTwo').offset().top;
            return (($(document).scrollTop() + $('#header').outerHeight(true)) >= top) && (($(document).scrollTop() + $('#header').outerHeight(true)) >= 1000);
        };
    
        $(window).on('resize scroll', function() {
            $('.jobColumnTwo').each(function() {
                if ($(this).jobColumnOneInViewport()) {
                    $('#skillMatcherBtnSticky').addClass("bh-survey-sticky-btn-2");
                } else if (!$(this).jobColumnOneInViewport()){
                    $('#skillMatcherBtnSticky').removeClass("bh-survey-sticky-btn-2");
                }
            });
            $('.jobColumnTwo').each(function() {
                if ($(this).jobColumnTwoInViewport()) {
                    $('#skillMatcherBtnSticky').addClass("bh-survey-sticky-btn-3");
                } else if (!$(this).jobColumnTwoInViewport()){
                    $('#skillMatcherBtnSticky').removeClass("bh-survey-sticky-btn-3");
                }
            });
        });
</script>

    function deleteFooter() {
        var footerRowTop = document.querySelector("#footerRowTop");
        footerRowTop.remove();
        var footerRowBottom = document.querySelector("#footerRowBottom");
        footerRowBottom.remove();
        var footerColumnsShell = document.querySelector("#footerColumnsShell");
        footerColumnsShell.remove();.
        var footerColumnsShellglobal= document.querySelector("#footerColumnsShellglobal");
        footerColumnsShellglobal.remove();
        var headersubmenu = document.querySelector(".lower.headersubmenu");
        headersubmenu.remove();
    }
    window.onload = deleteFooter;
</script>
<script type="text/javascript">
    function myFunction() {
        var topbar = document.querySelector(".nav-pills").lastChild;
        var langLink = document.querySelector(".languageselector");
        var langList = document.querySelector(".headerdropdown");
        var profile = document.querySelector(".profileWidget > a");
        var list1 = document.createElement("li");
        var list2 = document.createElement("li");

        list1.classList.add("custom-menu-item1");
        list2.classList.add("custom-menu-item2");
        list1.appendChild(langLink);
        list1.appendChild(langList);
        list2.appendChild(profile);

        topbar.after(list1);
        topbar.after(list2);

        var subMenu = document.querySelector(".lower.headersubmenu");
        subMenu.remove();
    }

            <script type="text/javascript">
            //<![CDATA[
                if (Cookies && !Cookies.get('rmk12')) {
                    $('.ukCookiePolicy').show();

                    $('#cookie-close').click(function () {
                        closeBanner();
                    });

                    $('#cookie-acknowledge').click(function () {
                        closeBanner(true);
                    });

                    /**
                     * Closes the cookie banner, optionally dropping a cookie to keep the banner from reappearing.
                     * @param {boolean=} bDropCookie - If true, a cookie will be dropped to prevent the banner from
                     *     being shown again.
                     */
                    function closeBanner(bDropCookie) {
                        if (bDropCookie) {
                            Cookies.set('rmk12', 1, {
                                expires: (function () {
                                    var i = new Date;
                                    i.setFullYear(i.getFullYear() + 30);
                                    return i;
                                }())
                            });
                        }

                        $('div.ukCookiePolicy').remove();

                        /* When the banner is removed, the fixed header may need to be resized. If there is no fixed
                        header, this event goes unhandled. Please see header.xhtml. */
                        $(document).trigger('resizeFixedHeader');

                        $("#diversion").focus();
                    }
                }
            //]]>
            </script>

                // This code is to deal with empty e-mail strings on back button clicks to the page when first logging in.
                $(window).on( "load", function () {
                    if (''.length && !j2w.SSO.getEmail().length) {
                        $.ajax({
                            type    : 'GET',
                            url     : '/services/security/email',
                            success : function (data) {
                                if (data.email.length) {
                                    j2w.SSO.setEmail(data.email);
                                }
                            }
                        });
                    }
                });

                        <script type="text/javascript">
                            //<![CDATA[
                            $(function() {
                                $('.emailsubscribe-button').click(function (e) {
                                    e.preventDefault();
                                    var $frequency = $('.subscribe-frequency').val();
                                    var rcmLoggedIn = false;
                                    var action = rcmLoggedIn ? 'alertCreate' : 'subscribe';
                                    var result = j2w.Agent.validateFrequency($frequency);
                                    if (!result.length) {
                                        j2w.TC.collectForCASWorkflow({
                                            "emailAddress": '',
                                            "action": action,
                                            "socialSrc": '',
                                            "frequency": $frequency
                                        });
                                    } else {
                                        if (j2w.Args.get('isResponsive')) {
                                            $('.frequency-error-message').html(result.concat('<br/>'));
                                            $('.frequency-error').removeClass('hidden');
                                        } else {
                                            alert(result.join('\n'));
                                        }
                                    }
                                });
                            });
                            //]]>
                        </script>
